She carefully observes patterns of movement before making decisions about which button(s) to press next; this teaches her cause-and-effect relationships between inputs (button presses) and outputs (object movements).

Lastly, Scene D illustrates another instance where she uses physical intuition in simulated scenarios involving mechanical devices with different shapes or textures on the floor that could affect her balance when walking. By analyzing these visual cues before stepping onto each shape, she can avoid tripping over them.

Overall, all four scenes depict various aspects of physical intuition being applied to navigate and interact effectively within both real-world environments (like a living room) as well as simulated ones.
